  uf_sigla character varying(2) NOT NULL,
  CONSTRAINT uf_pkey PRIMARY KEY (uf_codigo)
)
WITH (OIDS=FALSE);

CREATE TABLE cidade
(
  cid_codigo integer NOT NULL,
  cid_nome character varying(60) NOT NULL,
  uf_codigo integer NOT NULL,
  CONSTRAINT cidade_pkey PRIMARY KEY (cid_codigo),
  CONSTRAINT cidade_uf_codigo_fkey FOREIGN KEY (uf_codigo)
      REFERENCES uf (uf_codigo) MATCH SIMPLE
      ON UPDATE NO ACTION ON DELETE NO ACTION
)
WITH (OIDS=FALSE);

CREATE TABLE usuario
(
  usu_codigo integer NOT NULL,
  usu_nome character varying(100) NOT NULL,
  usu_login character varying(6) NOT NULL,
  usu_senha character varying(6) NOT NULL,
  CONSTRAINT usuario_pkey PRIMARY KEY (usu_codigo),
  CONSTRAINT usuario_usu_login_key UNIQUE (usu_login)
)
WITH (
  OIDS=FALSE
);
insert into usuario (usu_codigo, usu_nome, usu_login, usu_senha) values (1, 'Administrador', 'admin', 'admin');

CREATE TABLE aluno
(
  alu_codigo serial NOT NULL,
  alu_nome character varying(150) NOT NULL,
  alu_email character varying(150) NOT NULL,
  alu_senha character varying(10) NOT NULL,
  alu_endereco character varying(250) NOT NULL,
  alu_numero integer,
  alu_complemento character varying(25),
  alu_cep character varying(8) NOT NULL,
  cid_codigo integer NOT NULL,
  alu_data_nasc date NOT NULL,
  alu_cpf character varying(11) NOT NULL,
  CONSTRAINT aluno_pkey PRIMARY KEY (alu_codigo),
  CONSTRAINT aluno_cid_codigo_fkey FOREIGN KEY (cid_codigo)
      REFERENCES cidade (cid_codigo) MATCH SIMPLE
      ON UPDATE NO ACTION ON DELETE NO ACTION,
  CONSTRAINT aluno_alu_email_key UNIQUE (alu_email)
)
WITH (
  OIDS=FALSE
);


CREATE TABLE evento
(
  eve_codigo serial NOT NULL,
  eve_nome character varying(250) NOT NULL,
  eve_inicio date NOT NULL,
  eve_fim date NOT NULL,
  CONSTRAINT evento_pkey PRIMARY KEY (eve_codigo)
)
WITH (
  OIDS=FALSE
);

CREATE TABLE palestra
(
  pal_codigo serial NOT NULL,
  eve_codigo integer NOT NULL,
  pal_nome character varying(200) NOT NULL,
  pal_nr_inscritos_max integer NOT NULL,
  pal_descricao text NOT NULL,
  pal_data date NOT NULL,
  CONSTRAINT palestra_pkey PRIMARY KEY (pal_codigo),
  CONSTRAINT palestra_eve_codigo_fkey FOREIGN KEY (eve_codigo)
      REFERENCES evento (eve_codigo) MATCH SIMPLE
      ON UPDATE NO ACTION ON DELETE NO ACTION
)
WITH (
  OIDS=FALSE
);

CREATE TABLE instrutor
(
  ins_codigo serial NOT NULL,
  ins_nome character varying(200) NOT NULL,
  ins_curriculo text NOT NULL,
  CONSTRAINT instrutor_pkey PRIMARY KEY (ins_codigo)
)
WITH (
  OIDS=FALSE
);

CREATE TABLE palestra_instrutor
(
  pal_codigo integer NOT NULL,
  ins_codigo integer NOT NULL,
  CONSTRAINT palestra_instrutor_pkey PRIMARY KEY (pal_codigo, ins_codigo),
  CONSTRAINT palestra_instrutor_ins_codigo_fkey FOREIGN KEY (ins_codigo)
      REFERENCES instrutor (ins_codigo) MATCH SIMPLE
      ON UPDATE NO ACTION ON DELETE NO ACTION,
  CONSTRAINT palestra_instrutor_pal_codigo_fkey FOREIGN KEY (pal_codigo)
      REFERENCES palestra (pal_codigo) MATCH SIMPLE
      ON UPDATE NO ACTION ON DELETE NO ACTION
)
WITH (
  OIDS=FALSE
);

CREATE TABLE matricula
(
  mat_codigo serial NOT NULL,
  alu_codigo integer NOT NULL,
  eve_codigo integer NOT NULL,
  mat_confirmada boolean NOT NULL DEFAULT false,
  CONSTRAINT matricula_pkey PRIMARY KEY (mat_codigo),
  CONSTRAINT matricula_eve_codigo_fkey FOREIGN KEY (eve_codigo)
      REFERENCES evento (eve_codigo) MATCH SIMPLE
      ON UPDATE NO ACTION ON DELETE NO ACTION,
  CONSTRAINT matricula_alu_codigo_fkey FOREIGN KEY (alu_codigo)
      REFERENCES aluno (alu_codigo) MATCH SIMPLE
      ON UPDATE NO ACTION ON DELETE NO ACTION
)
WITH (
  OIDS=FALSE
);

CREATE TABLE matricula_palestra
(
  mat_codigo integer NOT NULL,
  pal_codigo integer NOT NULL,
  CONSTRAINT matricula_palestra_pkey PRIMARY KEY (mat_codigo, pal_codigo),
  CONSTRAINT matricula_palestra_mat_codigo_fkey FOREIGN KEY (mat_codigo)
      REFERENCES matricula (mat_codigo) MATCH SIMPLE
      ON UPDATE NO ACTION ON DELETE NO ACTION,
  CONSTRAINT matricula_palestra_pal_codigo_fkey FOREIGN KEY (pal_codigo)
      REFERENCES palestra (pal_codigo) MATCH SIMPLE
      ON UPDATE NO ACTION ON DELETE NO ACTION
)
WITH (
  OIDS=FALSE
);
